# Task
Determine if the given text contains explicit hate speech directed towards a particular race, ethnicity, religion, nationality, gender, or sexual orientation using aggressive and derogatory language designed to provoke hostility or belittle individuals within that group, or if it targets individuals or groups based on inherent characteristics such as race, religion, national origin, disability, sex, or sexual orientation through the use of slurs, dehumanizing descriptions, or incitements to violence against a particular group. ### Expert 0
Determine if the given text contains explicit hate speech directed towards a particular race, ethnicity, religion, nationality, gender, or sexual orientation using aggressive and derogatory language designed to provoke hostility or belittle individuals within that group. Anger or dissatisfaction that is not specifically targeted at a protected category should not be considered as hate speech. Does the following text qualify as hate speech?

### Expert 1
"Determine if the provided text includes hate speech. Hate speech is defined by hostile language, abusive remarks, or pejorative comments directed at individuals or groups due to immutable characteristics like race, religion, nationality, sex, sexual identity, disability, or military service. It also encompasses manifestations of intense negativity or disdain toward cultural rituals, festivals, or convictions linked to particular religions or nationalities. Instances involve overt advocacy for violence, prejudiced conduct, epithets, encouragement of detrimental behavior against a group, mockery of religious rites, or severe reproach of specific traditions or celebrations. However, robust criticism or dissatisfaction that does not attack or disrespect a group is not classified as hate speech."

### Expert 2
"Evaluate whether the text contains clear expressions of bias or animosity toward any protected group, which would categorize it as hate speech. Focus specifically on direct and unambiguous indications of hatred or contempt. Do not label as hate speech texts that employ sarcasm or general mockery, unless such content is explicitly targeted at a protected group."

# Task
Determine if the provided text includes explicit hate speech or clear expressions of bias or animosity toward any protected group, including race, ethnicity, religion, nationality, gender, sexual orientation, disability, or military service. Evaluate whether the text contains hostile language, abusive remarks, pejorative comments, or direct and unambiguous indications of hatred or contempt directed at individuals or groups because of these immutable characteristics. This also encompasses manifestations of intense negativity or disdain toward cultural rituals, festivals, or convictions linked to particular religions or nationalities, such as overt advocacy for violence, prejudiced conduct, epithets, encouragement of detrimental behavior against a group, mockery of religious rites, or severe reproach of specific traditions or celebrations. However, anger, dissatisfaction, robust criticism, sarcasm, or general mockery that do not specifically target or attack a protected category or group should not be considered as hate speech. Does the following text qualify as hate speech?
# Output format

NO explanations.
